CustomInfo: ConfigParam "Name=PlanRes" "Parent=Path Planning Settings" "Priority=Normal" "Type=double" "Desc=The resolution of the grid used for path planning in mm. It is best to use an integral fraction of the robot half width to allow for more free space in tight spaces. Smaller resolutions may let you plan through tight spaces, but will increase the computation load. Halving the resolution will raise the computation by a factor of 4." "Value=70" "Min=1"
CustomInfo: ConfigParam "Name=UseRadiusForPlan" "Parent=Path Planning Settings" "Priority=Normal" "Type=bool" "Desc=The path planner assumes that the shape of the robot is approximately a circle with a radius equal to half the robot width. Typical robots are oblong rather than circular in shape. Using the half width allows the planner to find paths through tight spots in the map like doors and narrow passages. This may cause such robots to get stuck when it tries to avoid unmapped obstacles in such tight spaces. To avoid such cases, it might be useful to make the path planner use the robot radius for path planning. This may prevent the robot from driving into tight spaces, but it also ensures that it will be able to drive in and out of any point in the path it plans." "Value=false"
CustomInfo: ConfigParam "Name=UseRearFraction" "Parent=Path Planning Settings" "Priority=Normal" "Type=double" "Desc=How far to extend the side clearances from the center of rotation to the rear of the robot. This is a multiple of the robot rear length. If the robot has rounded corners, then this value should typically be less than one. (For the LD and Lynx, the default is 0.5.) This reduces the likelihood that the robot will get stuck during path following when, otherwise, the rear corners would appear to clip obstacles during turns. This value should to be set to values larger than 1.0 on robots with rear safety zones." "Value=0.5" "Max=2"
